[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A critical security issue was detected by Jazzer’s file path traversal sanitizer    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         when fuzzing the `Expander` example from Apache Commons Compress. During a fuzzing  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         run, an input archive triggered a path traversal vulnerability, causing files to be [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         written to an unintended location under                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[35m/tmp/[0m[95mexpander-tmp[0m…[35m/output/q/r/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`. The Jazzer harness flagged this   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         as a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` at runtime.                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Issue Manifestation                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           The exception thrown is:                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         traversal: [35m/tmp/expander-tmp16285745061782862743/output/q/r/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           This indicates that an archive entry’s path caused the library to write outside   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the intended extraction directory.                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Vulnerability Type                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           File path traversal: an attacker-controlled path segment in an archive entry      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         allows escaping the target directory.                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Call Stack Highlights                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m. `FilePathTraversal.check` [1m([0mFilePathTraversal.jav[1;92ma:346[0m[1m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. `FilePathTraversal.checkPath` [1m([0mFilePathTraversal.jav[1;92ma:293[0m[1m)[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m3[0m. `FilePathTraversal.copyMismatchMvHook` [1m([0mFilePathTraversal.jav[1;92ma:211[0m[1m)[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m4[0m. `Expander.expand` [1m([0mExpander.jav[1;92ma:502[0m → [1;36m412[0m → [1;36m336[0m → [1;36m216[0m[1m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m5[0m. `ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` [1m([0mExpanderFuzzer.jav[1;92ma:52[0m[1m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Important Observations                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The sanitizer detected an output path that traverses directories                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`q/r/jazzer-traversal`[1m)[0m outside the intended sandbox.                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The vulnerability arises during the file-copy or rename phase                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`copyMismatchMvHook`[1m)[0m.                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • Multiple overloads of `Expander.expand` are involved, suggesting a common       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         path‐handling routine.                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Code Areas for Investigation                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m. The path‐validation logic in `FilePathTraversal.check` and `checkPath`.        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. The move/copy hook in `FilePathTraversal.copyMismatchMvHook`.                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m3[0m. The implementation of `Expander.expand` [1m([0mall overloads[1m)[0m, especially how it     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         translates archive entry names into file system paths.                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m4[0m. Any helper methods that join or normalize paths before extraction.             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Note on the Harness                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           The `ExpanderFuzzer` harness merely exercises the `Expander` code; it is not the  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         root cause but serves as the entry point that exposed the traversal issue.          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Initial Issue Log                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:            throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparentPath, name, outputFile[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:        return outputFile;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Identify Root Cause**[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The vulnerability stems from the default implementation of [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It merely does  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         Path outputFile = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m throw IOException [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     but fails to:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Normalize backslashes [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`\`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m used as separators on Windows.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Detect drive-letter prefixes like `C:\…`.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Prevent entry names beginning with `[0m[35m/[0m[39m` or `\` from being treated as absolute[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpaths.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - As a result, entry names such as `\..\evil.txt` or [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`C:\windows\system32\bad.dll` bypass the check and are written outside the target [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Patch Location**[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - File: `src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Method: `default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal Path parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Strategy to Harden `resolveIn`**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. **Sanitize the raw entry name**  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Read `String name = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Replace all backslashes with forward slashes:  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            `String sanitized = [0m[1;35mname.replace[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'\\', '[0m[35m/[0m[39m'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - If `sanitized` starts with `[0m[35m/[0m[39m`, reject: throws `[0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Illegal entry [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mname: "[0m[39m + name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - If it matches a Windows drive-letter prefix `^[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mA-Za-z[0m[1;39m][0m[39m:`, reject similarly.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. **Split into segments and re-build safely**  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Initialize `Path result = parentPath;`  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Loop over `for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mString segment : [0m[1;35msanitized.split[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"/"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • Skip empty or `[0m[32m"."[0m[39m` segments.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • If `[0m[32m".."[0m[39m`, then  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             – If `[0m[1;35mresult.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, throw `[0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Entry escapes [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mtarget dir: "[0m[39m + name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             – Else `result = [0m[1;35mresult.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • Otherwise `result = [0m[1;35mresult.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39msegment[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. **Final Safety Net**  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Optionally call `result = [0m[1;35mresult.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Verify `[0m[1;35mresult.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` one more time; if not, throw.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. **Return** `result`.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Preserve Existing Logic**[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We still throw `IOException` on invalid names, matching existing `Zip slip` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All valid relative paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwith `[0m[32m"."[0m[39m`, nested directories, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are still [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msupported.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We do not alter any code in `Expander`, the fuzzer harness, or any other [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mutilities.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Implementation Steps**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `ArchiveEntry.java`.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Replace the existing `default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` implementation[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith the hardened algorithm above.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Ensure imports if needed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnone beyond `java.nio.file.Path` and [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`java.io.IOException`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Recompile and run existing test suite—verify no regressions.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Run the `ExpanderFuzzer` harness to confirm the path-traversal input is now [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mblocked by our new checks [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuzzer should no longer reach the vulnerable [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile-write[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Justification**[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Security:** Explicitly blocks both Unix and Windows traversal vectors [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mbackslashes, drive letters, leading slashes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Compatibility:** Legitimate entries [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. `dir/sub/file.txt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munaffected.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Minimal Scope:** Only modifies the `resolveIn` helper; no changes to [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction logic, I/O APIs, or test code.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Defense-in-Depth:** Adds segment-by-segment validation on top of the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting `[0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` & `[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` pattern.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. **Potential Side-Effects & Mitigation**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Archives containing entries with a leading slash or drive-letter prefix will [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnow throw an `IOException`. These archives were already invalid under standard [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“zip-slip” safety guidelines. If certain use-cases legitimately need leading-slash [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpaths, they must pre-sanitize entry names upstream.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other code paths are affected because only this one default method is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanged.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. **References**[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar segment-based path resolution is used in other libraries [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., OWASP [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecure-coding recipes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The existing test harness for `Expander` will confirm that the fix blocks the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalicious input without altering normal extraction behavior.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         entry names, rejects absolute and Windows‐drive prefixes, manually processes “..”   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         segments, and enforces that the final path remains under the target directory.      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         After rebuilding with this patch, the same Jazzer exception is still raised when    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         running the Expander fuzzer, indicating that the attempted fix did not fully        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         eliminate the path traversal condition.                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. Initial Issue                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - A Jazzer security sanitizer detected a “File path traversal” during the        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         expansion of archive entries under `[35m/tmp/[0m…[35m/output/q/r/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`.            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The stack trace shows the violation is caught by `[1;35mFilePathTraversal.check[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         → [1;35mcopyMismatchMvHook[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` in the Jazzer sanitizer, and originates in               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`, ultimately   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         invoked by the fuzzer harness `ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`.                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - This indicates that certain entry names in the archive permit escaping the     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         intended output directory, a classic zip‐slip vulnerability.                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. Patch Attempt                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The patch modifies `[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1m([0mPath parentPath[1m)[0m`:                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Replaces `[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1m([0mname[1m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` with a multi‐step sanitizer. [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Converts backslashes to forward slashes, rejects names starting with `[35m/[0m` or  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         a drive‐letter prefix.                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Splits the sanitized name on `[35m/[0m`, skipping empty or “.” segments, handling   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         “..” by moving up one directory [1m([0mbut throwing if it would escape the root[1m)[0m.         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Resolves and normalizes the final `Path` and rechecks that it still starts   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         with `parentPath`, throwing an `IOException` otherwise.                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The patch diff can be re-applied by replacing the body of                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `ArchiveEntry.resolveIn` with the new code block shown in the patch attempt.        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. Result After Patch                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Running the Expander fuzzer again produces the same Jazzer exception:          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              “File path traversal: [35m/tmp/[0m…[35m/output/q/r/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m …”                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The stack trace is unchanged, demonstrating that the attempted sanitization in [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `resolveIn` does not prevent all forms of path‐traversal exploitation reachable by  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the fuzzer.                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. Further Investigation Points                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The implementation of `[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` [1m([0mlines [1;36m216[0m, [1;36m336[0m, [1;36m412[0m, [1;36m502[0m[1m)[0m and    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         how it uses `ArchiveEntry.resolveIn` or other path computations.                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Any alternative code paths for entry extraction that bypass `resolveIn`, for   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         example custom handling of directory vs file entries.                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Interaction between archive formats [1m([0mZIP, TAR, etc.[1m)[0m and name normalization    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         logic upstream of `ArchiveEntry`.                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Whether symbolic link entries or special entry types are handled elsewhere,    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         allowing escape.                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The harness-to-library boundary: how the fuzzer input drives archive creation  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         and which archive APIs are invoked before reaching the sanitizer.                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ---                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         No speculation has been made about the root cause beyond the observable             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         path‐traversal checks failing to cover all malformed entry names. The points above  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         outline where to look next to build a comprehensive understanding of the remaining  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         zip‐slip issues.                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m485[0m[39m:                    link = [0m[1;35mparent.relativize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlink.getFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m486[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m487[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mFiles.isRegularFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlink[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && ![0m[1;35mFiles.isSymbolicLink[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlink[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m488[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mFiles.createSymbolicLink[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlink, target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m489[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m490[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m! [0m[1;35mzae.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m491[0m[39m:                Path target = [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m492[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m493[0m[39m:                    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m-> '%s'"[0m[39m,[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m494[0m[39m:                            targetDirectory, [0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, target[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m495[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m496[0m[39m:                Path parent = [0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory, target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m497[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m! [0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m498[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mparent.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m499[0m[39m:                    target = [0m[1;35mparent.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m500[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m501[0m[39m:                try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35marchive.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mzae[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m502[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mFiles.copy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m503[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m504[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m505[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Reapply and preserve the hardened `[0m[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` implementation [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom the last patch attempt:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Normalize backslashes to forward slashes.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Reject leading “[0m[35m/[0m[39m” or Windows‐drive prefixes.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Manually process “.” and “..” segments, throwing if traversal would escape.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After building the path, normalize and verify it still starts with the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintended parent.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Centralize all archive‐entry path resolution in `Expander` onto the `resolveIn` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault method, eliminating any bypasses:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mZipFile archive, Path targetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m470[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m505[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Symlink branch [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mzae.isUnixSymlink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          • Replace[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              Path link = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            with[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              Path link = [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mArchiveEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m zae[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          • Remove manual `relativize` adjustment and duplicate startsWith checks.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          • Use `[0m[1;35mlink.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for `[0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, then create [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe symlink.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - File branch [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`![0m[1;35mzae.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          • Replace[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              Path target = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            with[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              Path target = [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mArchiveEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m zae[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          • Remove both the manual startsWith check and the secondary [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparent‐relativize hack.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          • Immediately call `[0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory, target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcopy.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Repeat the same replacement in any other `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` overloads [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., TAR, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ArchiveInputStream`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that perform their own `resolve`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`normalize` and startsWith [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecks.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Ensure `[0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is only responsible for directory creation, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot path sanitization.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Run existing unit tests and fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to verify:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Zip‐slip sanitizer errors are no longer raised.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No existing archive‐expansion behavior is broken.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJustification:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The root cause is that the ZIP‐based expansion code never invoked [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ArchiveEntry.resolveIn`, so the prior patch had no effect on that branch.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- By routing all path computations through the hardened `resolveIn` method, we [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguarantee consistent slash‐normalization, “..” handling, absolute‐path rejection, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand anchored result checks.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This preserves existing functionality [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwe still create parent directories and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcopy data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m but prevents any unnormalized or crafted entry name from escaping the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtarget directory.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Similar logic already exists for non‐ZIP codepaths via `resolveIn`; centralizing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavoids duplication and future drift.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Side‐effects are minimal: only path resolution logic changes, not file copying or[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer harness. All existing tests and fuzzers continue to operate with the same [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAPI.[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The exception trace shows the sanitizer rejecting a malicious entry path in [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FilePathTraversal.check`, invoked from `Expander.copyMismatchMvHook` and [0m          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The issue indicates that archive entries with “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” or absolute paths can escape [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe intended extraction directory, triggering a security violation.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mKey Observations  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The vulnerability is triggered before any application logic misbehaves: it is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcaught by the Jazzer sanitizer as a critical security issue.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The stack trace pinpoints the problem to how `Expander` resolves entry names into[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No runtime or functional log is present beyond the fuzzer crash, but the failure [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. In `[0m[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min [0m                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Removed the naive `[0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` approach.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Introduced manual splitting of the entry name on forward slashes, rejecting [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - At the end, re-normalize and verify that the resolved path still lies under [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parentPath`.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replaced direct calls to `[0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith calls to the new `[0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method, casting `zae` to the library’s [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ArchiveEntry` interface.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Removed some ad-hoc parent-directory checks around symlink creation and file [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction, relying instead on `resolveIn` to prevent path traversal.  [0m             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCompilation Result  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The compiler reports “’else’ without ‘if’” at line [0m[1;36m487[0m[39m, and numerous “class, [0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbroken block structure [0m[1;39m([0m[39mprobably unbalanced `[0m[1;39m{[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` around the new `if [0m                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                 at [1;35mExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1m([0mExpanderFuzzer.jav[1;92ma:52[0m[1m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         DEDUP_TOKEN: 7bb3f9683ba8f59b                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         An Apache Commons Compress fuzzer [1m([0mExpanderFuzzer[1m)[0m triggered a Jazzer security      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         issue for file path traversal when expanding archive entries outside the intended   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         output directory. To address this, a patch was introduced:                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - In `ArchiveEntry.java`, a new `[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1m([0mPath[1m)[0m` method replaces the simple        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mresolve[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` approach with manual segment-by-segment resolution,         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         sanitizing backslashes, rejecting absolute and drive-letter paths, and explicitly   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         handling “.” and “..” segments.                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - In `Expander.java`, calls to `[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1m([0m…[1m)[0m` were replaced with      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1m([0m[1m([0mArchiveEntry[1m)[0m zae[1m)[0m[1;35m.resolveIn[0m[1m([0mtargetDirectory[1m)[0m` for both symlinks and file        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         entries, and `[1;35mcreateParentDirectory[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` was invoked to ensure directories exist   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         before writing or linking.                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         After applying the patch, the build failed with five compilation errors in          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `Expander.java` [1m([0m`class, interface, or enum expected`[1m)[0m, indicating a syntactic      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         mismatch—most likely misplaced or missing braces in the modified code block.        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Initial Issue                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The Jazzer fuzzer reported a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path traversal`   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         exception while running `[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`.                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The vulnerable code path involved `[1;35mFilePathTraversal.copyMismatchMvHook[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         detecting that a resolved output path lay outside its parent directory, pointing to [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         a classic “zip slip” scenario.                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Important Observations                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The failure arises during archive expansion of entries whose names contain        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         traversal sequences or absolute paths.                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The existing code used `[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1m([0mname[1m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` plus a `startsWith` [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         check, which was deemed insufficient by the fuzzer harness.                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Patch Attempt                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. **ArchiveEntry.java**                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Removed naïve `[1;35mresolve[0m[1m([0mname[1m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` logic.                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Added `[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1m([0mPath parentPath[1m)[0m` default method:                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Replaces backslashes with forward slashes.                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Rejects names starting with “[35m/[0m” or matching a Windows drive-letter pattern.  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Splits on “[35m/[0m” and iteratively resolves segments, guarding against escaping   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the `parentPath`.                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Performs a final `[1;35mnormalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` and `startsWith` check before returning.      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. **Expander.java** [1m([0maround lines [1;36m477[0m–[1;36m520[0m[1m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - For Unix symlinks: replaced                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              `Path link = [1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1m([0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m;`                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              with                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              `Path link = [1m([0m[1m([0mArchiveEntry[1m)[0m zae[1m)[0m[1;35m.resolveIn[0m[1m([0mtargetDirectory[1m)[0m;`                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - For regular files: similarly replaced manual resolve and normalize steps with  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `resolveIn`.                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Ensured parent directories by calling `[1;35mcreateParentDirectory[0m[1m([0mtargetDirectory,  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         linkOrTarget[1m)[0m` before invoking `Files.createSymbolicLink` or `Files.copy`.          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Patch Application Logs                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Maven build begins recompilation, but hits errors in `Expander.java` at lines     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m519[0m, [1;36m522[0m, [1;36m524[0m, and [1;36m526[0m:                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           “class, interface, or enum expected.”                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - These errors indicate that the modified section has an unmatched brace or stray   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         tokens outside any method or class body.                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Areas for Further Investigation                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The edited block in `Expander.java`: verify that all opening `[1m{[0m` and closing `[1m}[0m`  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         braces align, and that the patched code is inside the correct method                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`[1;35mexpand[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`[1m)[0m rather than inserted at class scope.                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The import and cast to `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.ArchiveEntry`:      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         confirm that the correct interface is referenced and available in this context.     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The interaction between `[1;35mcreateParentDirectory[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` and the new `resolveIn`      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         logic: ensure directory creation calls match the intended targets.                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Remaining uses of `resolve`[35m/[0m`normalize` elsewhere in `Expander.java` or related   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         classes that might still permit traversal outside the target directory.             [2m                [0m
